---

### Term: H6944G (qo.desh) | mti_term_id=904 | gloss: holiness | 286 verses

**Gloss note:** qo.desh is the substantive/noun form — the holiness, the sanctuary, the holy thing/place. Corpus of 286 verses covers the full range from cultic/spatial to inner-moral. Filter applied strictly at term level. Many verses in this corpus are purely cultic (sanctuary, holy vessels, holy times, shekel of the sanctuary) with no inner-being engagement for this term's specific use.

**CLASSIFICATION BLOCK**

```
GROUP 904-001
context_description: Term names holiness as the inner moral character and set-apart orientation by which the person is consecrated to God — the quality of the person's inner life that corresponds to God's own holiness and is required for approach to him
notes: null

GROUP 904-002
context_description: Term names the person's inner response — reverence, worship, and desire — evoked by encountering the holiness of God in his sanctuary or name
notes: null

GROUP 904-003
context_description: Term names the Spirit's holiness as the divine inner presence that grieves over human rebellion and is placed within the people by God — the inner holy presence as relational reality
notes: null
```

---

## Registry 77 — honesty

---

### Term: H6662 (tsad.diq) | mti_term_id=3246 | gloss: righteous | 184 verses

**Gloss note:** Adjective — the righteous person; also used of God's character and legal verdicts. Core inner-being vocabulary: righteousness as the moral character of the whole inner life. The vast majority of verses relevant; set-asides limited to bare divine-attribute statements.

**CLASSIFICATION BLOCK**

```
GROUP 3246-001
context_description: Term names the righteous person's inner moral character — the constitutive orientation of the whole inner being toward what is right before God and others, expressed in conduct, desire, speech, and relationship
notes: null

GROUP 3246-002
context_description: Term names righteousness as the standard by which God tests and vindicates — the inner moral condition that God sees, approves, and rewards, and which may be abandoned
notes: null

GROUP 3246-003
context_description: Term names the inner response of the righteous person toward God — the orientation of trust, joy, and praise that flows from knowing God is righteous
notes: null
```

---

### Term: H6666 (tse.da.qah) | mti_term_id=911 | gloss: righteousness | 148 verses

**Gloss note:** Noun — righteousness as a quality, act, or status. Core inner-being vocabulary. All 148 verses essentially relevant; set-asides minimal (bare divine attribute statements).

**CLASSIFICATION BLOCK**

```
GROUP 911-001
context_description: Term names righteousness as the inner moral character of the person — the quality of being in right relationship with God and others, expressed in just conduct, faithful dealing, and integrity
notes: null

GROUP 911-002
context_description: Term names righteousness as the status credited to or vindicated in the person by God — the inner moral standing of the person before God, whether through faithfulness or divine imputation
notes: null

GROUP 911-003
context_description: Term names righteousness as the divine character quality that the person receives, longs for, and responds to — God's own righteousness as gift, as stream of salvation, and as the ground of the person's inner hope and exultation
notes: null
```

### Term: H5027 (na.vat) | mti_term_id=2617 | gloss: to look | 67 verses

**Gloss note:** Expression term (Section 3.4 applies). The act of looking passes the filter when it plausibly originates in an inner state or discloses an inner orientation. Three materially distinct groups: looking to God (inner orientation), looking that discloses inner attitude, and divine looking toward humanity.

**Structured classification blocks:**
- 2617-001: *Term names the inner act of looking to God — the orientation of the person's gaze toward God in prayer, trust, hope, or longing* | Anchor: Psa 34:5 | Related: Gen 19:26, Exo 3:6, Exo 33:8, Num 12:8, Num 21:9, 1Ki 18:43, Job 6:19, 35:5, Psa 119:6, 119:15, 119:18, Isa 42:18, 51:1, 51:2, 51:6, 63:15, 64:9, 66:2, Hab 1:5, Zec 12:10, Jon 2:4
